limitations under the License.\n */\npackage org.apache.camel.component.fix;\n\nimport org.apache.camel.Exchange;\nimport org.apache.camel.Processor;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.DefaultConsumer;\nimport org.slf4j.Logger;\nimport org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;\nimport quickfix.Application;\nimport quickfix.DoNotSend;\nimport quickfix.FieldNotFound;\nimport quickfix.IncorrectDataFormat;\nimport quickfix.IncorrectTagValue;\nimport quickfix.Message;\nimport quickfix.RejectLogon;\nimport quickfix.Session;\nimport quickfix.SessionID;\nimport quickfix.SessionSettings;\nimport quickfix.SocketAcceptor;\nimport quickfix.UnsupportedMessageType;\nimport quickfix.field.MsgType;\nimport quickfix.field.SenderCompID;\nimport quickfix.field.TargetCompID;\n\n/**\n * The FIX consumer receives inbound FIX messages and feeds them into Camel routes.\n */\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer implements Application {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixConsumer.class);\n\n    private SocketAcceptor acceptor;\n\n    public FixConsumer(FixEndpoint endpoint, Processor processor) {\n        super(endpoint, processor);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixEndpoint getEndpoint() {\n        return (FixEndpoint) super.getEndpoint();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        super.doStart();\n\n        FixConfiguration config = getEndpoint().getConfiguration();\n        SessionSettings settings = buildSessionSettings(config);\n\n        quickfix.DefaultMessageFactory messageFactory = new quickfix.DefaultMessageFactory();\n        quickfix.FileStoreFactory storeFactory = new quickfix.FileStoreFactory(settings);\n        quickfix.ScreenLogFactory logFactory = new quickfix.ScreenLogFactory(settings);\n\n        acceptor = new SocketAcceptor(this, storeFactory, settings, logFactory, messageFactory);\n        acceptor.start();\n\n        LOG.info(\"FIX acceptor started for session {}\", getEndpoint().getSessionID());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        if (acceptor != null) {\n            acceptor.stop();\n            acceptor = null;\n            LOG.info(\"FIX acceptor stopped for session {}\", getEndpoint().getSessionID());\n        }\n\n        super.doStop();\n    }\n\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // QuickFIX/J Application callbacks\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    @Override\n    public void onCreate(SessionID sessionId) {\n        LOG.debug(\"FIX session created: {}\", sessionId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onLogon(SessionID sessionId) {\n        LOG.info(\"FIX session logged on: {}\", sessionId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onLogout(SessionID sessionId) {\n        LOG.info(\"FIX session logged out: {}\", sessionId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void toAdmin(Message message, SessionID sessionId) {\n        // no-op: admin messages sent by the engine\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void fromAdmin(Message message, SessionID sessionId)\n            throws FieldNotFound, IncorrectDataFormat, IncorrectTagValue, RejectLogon {\n        // no-op: admin messages received from counterparty\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void toApp(Message message, SessionID sessionId) throws DoNotSend {\n        // no-op: application messages sent by this endpoint\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void fromApp(Message message, SessionID sessionId)\n            throws FieldNotFound, IncorrectDataFormat, IncorrectTagValue, UnsupportedMessageType {\n        Exchange exchange = createExchange(false);\n        try {\n            String msgType = message.getHeader().getString(MsgType.FIELD);\n            String sender = message.getHeader().getString(SenderCompID.FIELD);\n            String target = message.getHeader().getString(TargetCompID.FIELD);\n\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, msgType);\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, sessionId.toString());\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, sender);\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, target);\n            exchange.getIn().setBody(message);\n\n            getProcessor().process(exchange);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            getExceptionHandler().handleException(\"Error processing FIX message.\", exchange, e);\n        } finally {\n            releaseExchange(exchange, false);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Helpers\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    private SessionSettings buildSessionSettings(FixConfiguration config) throws Exception {\n        if (config.getConfigFile() != null) {\n            return new SessionSettings(config.getConfigFile());\n        }\n\n        // Build minimal settings programmatically\n        SessionSettings settings = \"fix:sessionID\", category = {Category.NETWORKING})\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint {\n    @UriPath String sessionID;\n    @UriParam FixConfiguration configuration;\n    public Producer createProducer() { return new FixProducer(this); }\n    public Consumer createConsumer(Processor processor) { return new FixConsumer(this, processor); }\n}\n```\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java (new)\nExtends `DefaultConsumer`, implements QuickFIX/J `Application` interface. `doStart()` builds\n`SessionSettings` (from file or programmatically), creates a `SocketAcceptor` and starts it.\n`fromApp()` callback dispatches incoming FIX `Message` objects as Camel exchanges with\n`CamelFixMessageType`, `CamelFixSessionID`, `CamelFixSenderCompID`, `CamelFixTargetCompID` headers.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixProducer.java (new)\nExtends `DefaultAsyncProducer`. `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` extracts a QuickFIX/J `Message`\nfrom the exchange body, resolves the target `SessionID` (from header or endpoint URI), and calls\n`Session.sendToTarget(message, sessionId)`.\n\n### Service descriptor files (new)\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component.properties`\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/org/apache/camel/component/fix/fix.json`\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\nThe camel-fix component integrates the QuickFIX/J library (v2.3.1) — the standard Java FIX engine —\nwith Apache Camel's routing infrastructure.\n\n**FIX Protocol**: FIX (Financial Information eXchange) is the industry standard for securities\ntrading messages. Sessions are identified by a triple (BeginString, SenderCompID, TargetCompID).\nThe URI path (`fix:FIX.4.4:MYCO->BROKER`) encodes this session identity.\n\n**Component Design**:\n- `FixComponent` is a thin factory that creates `FixEndpoint` instances, following the standard\n  `DefaultComponent` pattern seen throughout Camel.\n- `FixConfiguration` is a separate POJO (annotated with `@UriParams`) following the pattern used\n  by multi-param components. This keeps endpoint properties cleanly separated.\n- `FixEndpoint` follows `DefaultEndpoint` convention with `@UriEndpoint` metadata annotation.\n\n**Consumer**: `FixConsumer` acts as a QuickFIX/J `Application` (the FIX engine callback interface).\nIt creates a `SocketAcceptor` (server mode) that listens for incoming FIX connections. When a FIX\napplication message arrives via `fromApp()`, it is wrapped in a Camel `Exchange` and dispatched to\nthe route processor. Session lifecycle events (logon/logoff) are logged but not routed.\n\nWhen `configFile` is set, the `SessionSettings` are loaded from the QuickFIX/J properties file\n(the standard approach for production use). When not set, settings are built programmatically\nfrom the `FixConfiguration` fields.\n\n**Producer**: `FixProducer` extends `DefaultAsyncProducer` and implements `process(Exchange,\nAsyncCallback)`. `src/generated/resources/META-INF/org/apache/camel/component/fix/fix.json`\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\nThe camel-fix component integrates the QuickFIX/J library (v2.3.1) — the standard Java FIX engine —\nwith Apache Camel's routing infrastructure.\n\n**FIX Protocol**: FIX (Financial Information eXchange) is the industry standard for securities\ntrading messages. Sessions are identified by a triple (BeginString, SenderCompID, TargetCompID).\nThe URI path (`fix:FIX.4.4:MYCO->BROKER`) encodes this session identity.\n\n**Component Design**:\n- `FixComponent` is a thin factory that creates `FixEndpoint` instances, following the standard\n  `DefaultComponent` pattern seen throughout Camel.\n- `FixConfiguration` is a separate POJO (annotated with `@UriParams`) following the pattern used\n  by multi-param components. This keeps endpoint properties cleanly separated.\n- `FixEndpoint` follows `DefaultEndpoint` convention with `@UriEndpoint` metadata annotation.\n\n**Consumer**: `FixConsumer` acts as a QuickFIX/J `Application` (the FIX engine callback interface).\nIt creates a `SocketAcceptor` (server mode) that listens for incoming FIX connections. When a FIX\napplication message arrives via `fromApp()`, it is wrapped in a Camel `Exchange` and dispatched to\nthe route processor. Session lifecycle events (logon/logoff) are logged but not routed.\n\nWhen `configFile` is set, the `SessionSettings` are loaded from the QuickFIX/J properties file\n(the standard approach for production use). When not set, settings are built programmatically\nfrom the `FixConfiguration` fields.\n\n**Producer**: `FixProducer` extends `DefaultAsyncProducer` and implements `process(Exchange,\nAsyncCallback)`. It expects the exchange body to contain a QuickFIX/J `Message` object and\ncalls `Session.sendToTarget()` to dispatch it through the FIX engine's session layer.\nThe target session can be overridden at runtime via the `CamelFixSessionID` header.\n\n**Integration**: The module is registered in `components/pom.xml` in alphabetical order\n(between `camel-file-watch` and `camel-flatpack`). Service discovery metadata is provided in\n`src/generated/resources` following the convention of all other Camel components.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
